doing what you love is amazing but not easy working for yourself has wonderful benefits but has a flip side as well and can be difficult and even scary at times not having a boss to check your work or there to notice if you arrive on time doesn t mean you don t have a responsibility to your clients having an extra million distractions because you work from home is no easy challenge either hello procrastination what i m gaining a big lesson in is that while i m not always inspired to work i must remain disciplined day in day out discipline is important across the board right for all of us but if you are someone who is in a creative field it can be just one more very tough piece of the puzzle i don t always feel creative or inspired i can t see what i need to in a particular space of time most days i m changing in and out of paint clothes numerous times a day which includes these lovely pink slippers i wear in the outside studio because sometimes the rest of life requires you to be in non torn paint covered clothes nonetheless i have to treat it like a job which means staying disciplined and trying to get in the studio and find the flow even when i don t think it will b there a lot of times i m surprised what happens because well i just showed up are you doing what you love is it your main job or a side hustle if it s not what would that dream job be share in the comments

available parisian delight study 24x24 grease pencil acrylic on gallery thick canvas available now for 925 over 40 off was 1650 cad this study was begun back in 2015 for a show at in port dover but at the time i was compelled to leave it unfinished i went on to complete a much larger painting based from those photos for the show there was something i loved dearly about this one seeing so many of its initial stages exposed it s raw drawing marks with loose of colour the beginning that helped create more dimension the pop from a few highlights and the of the lemon meringue from the much loved urban parisian bakery all against ruby red lips it actually hung in my port dover studio for a few years it was a daily reminder to me to to learn to love again the raw stages of my work it was only this past year i finally took it down having since moved to st thomas and allowed myself to add just a few more strokes to make it complete it was then featured in a show i had this past spring at gallery 1051 in hamilton it s a favourite of mine for its subject its memories it s drawing elements the hours of just learning to try and understand why i couldn t bring myself to finish it everything about this painting is about the slow contemplation of pleasure how we should not be so quick about it instant is a cruel joke what we truly desire is long pleasures edges black ready to hang available now these prices will only be reduced for a limited time shipping is available in and the rest of the respecting the of the human form allows us to embrace the depths of our soul and in the depths of our own sensuality gmail com http www com http www facebook com

wat arun ratchawararam ratchawaramahawihan thai or wat arun thai pronunciation w t arun temple of dawn is a buddhist temple wat in bangkok yai district of bangkok thailand on the thonburi west bank of the chao phraya river the temple derives its name from the hindu god aruna often personified as the radiations of the rising sun wat arun is among the best known of thailand 's landmark the first light of the morning reflects off the surface of the temple with pearly iridescence although the temple had existed since at least the seventeenth century its distinctive prang spires were built in the early nineteenth century during the reign of king rama ii cr

how to work on your squat follow fit for daily fitness and health content save this to review later tag a friend who needs to see this increasing your range of motion is crucial for overall health and future movement as you age this squat pose is a great practice to take upon before your lower body training before you go to bed and right when you wake up the goal is to have our full foot planted on the floor with knees driving out over feet and trying our best to get our bum to the floor if it is tough to get into this position start by adding heel lifts to allow for more range of motion and if it is still a struggle start by sitting on a lower stool or chair foam rolling t spine mobility and hip mobility stretches are great prior to improve this movement try to hold down this squat position for time and increase the time every day eventually you will be able to watch tv study and hang out in this position for as long you want this position is especially important for athletes who s range of motion can be limited due to tightness due to sport activity get them squatting everyday let me know what you think in the comments below caption by fit content by

finale from the previous post via for the homemade spice add all of the ingredients to a small bowl and stir to mix for the spicy killer garlic dill pickles prepare your jars and lids for canning i run my jars through the to and remove them while still warm in a large stock pot bring the water and salt to a simmer to each jar add 2 3 tablespoons of spice 2 3 fronds and stalks of dried dill week 2 3 thai red peppers depending on your preference and 4 5 whole garlic cloves to each jar pack the cucumbers whole or sliced into the jars so they are tight but are n't damaged in the process the cucumbers should sit below the neck of the jar pour the into the jars leaving 1 2 inch headspace and just covering the cucumbers wipe the of the jars and use tongs to place the lids and rings that have been sterilized in water on top of the jars avoid touching the lids where they sit on the jars with your fingers to avoid process in a water bath for 10 minutes then remove the jars from the pot and allow them to cool on the counter as the jars cool you will hear them pop as they seal sealed jars should feel solid when tapped and be in shape store in a dry cool place pickles will be ready to try in about 7 10 days but get even better over time they can be stored for up to 1

are you a tea chai person if yes then how about enjoying this monsoon with a sip of boricha or barley tea it 's with we have got you korea 's favorite tea boricha boricha or barley tea is a roasted grain based infusion made from barley which is a staple across east asian regions like the and it has a flavor with slight bitter in korea the tea is consumed either hot or cold often taking the place of drinking water in many homes and restaurants benefits of korean barley tea 1 is caffeine free and there s no known side affects so you can drink as much as you like any time of the day 2 can help with digestion 3 can help with weight loss 4 can help control blood sugar level you can find boricha at premium tea shops or even at korean restaurants in india pic credits owners have been tagged in the pictures which is your favorite tea let us know get k amazed

wine of the day allegrini palazzo della torre 2016 producer of this valpolicella is allegrini located in in the heart of the valpolicella district in the veneto region of the northern part of italy this is one of the oldest vineyards in the area going back some 400 years they have perfected the art of to an almost level this is one of the wines that has made allegrini famous throughout the world the surrounds villa della torre a full bodied red wine that has an ageing potential of at least ten years the blend is the historic combination of and with the addition of a small quantity of the result is a velvety well balanced red wine that offers mature fruit 40 30 25 5 deep ruby red nose of cherries plums and spices on the palate it is elegant and well balanced with a good structure delicate rounded and good finish tech notes form the producer the fresh grapes were de and pressed in september while the dried grapes the same process in the second half of december fermentation in temperature controlled stainless steel tanks fermentation temperature and duration 1st fermentation 25 29 c 77 84 f 10 days 2nd fermentation 8 22 c 46 72 f approx 15 days fermentation in mid april in ageing 15 months in second use oak blended together for 2 months and then bottle aged for 7 months we had this delicious valpolicella with grilled beef and wonderful a perfect companion to steaks pastas traditional plates and the like

sanskar kendra sanskar kendra is an indian cultural center in ahmedabad which houses two museums famous for its building designed by celebrated architect le corbusier the building takes its name from sanskar kendra the first major of ahmedabad despite the construction being in rather bad conditions and needing major maintenance works and updates the museum is still worth a visit because of its historical importance completed in the home of the museums was designed in the early 50s as part of a larger development which also included the local mill owners association headquarters and two private houses villa and villa roughly in the same period le corbusier was designing the urban development of the city of chandigarh punjab le corbusier designed the museum with a great attention to the local conditions therefore adding an array of sun shading systems intensive planting and a roof equipped with 45 water each with a surface of 540 square feet and 13 foot deep to the hot climate of ahmedabad the museum is designed upon a 23 23 feet grid marked by an array of thin reinforced concrete columns the 11 feet high le corbusier also paid a special attention to natural light therefore the whole building is by a balance between sunlight and shade with deep concrete and brick clad where sky light shade and water are mixed together in a ensemble picture by

the most popular excuse people use for not focusing on their health is time the only acceptable excuse is family loved ones sick injured we all have the same 24hr in a day we make time for the things that are important to us we put aside the things that aren t it s that simple we don t need to train 7 hours a week to see results training 20 30 minutes a day is long enough to help you stay fit time is just an excuse we use because we don t want to do the work it s that simple the thing is you re either going to make time for your health now by eating clean and taking care of your body or you re going to make time for doctors appointments later when your health goes to shit time is just an excuse it s just something we put into our heads when we don t want to do something we need to our minds to stop thinking this way this is holly and are parents of two beautiful girls the girls play soccer basketball softball field hockey etc basically anything they can get involved in they play and who has to get them there yes holly and joe they both work full time jobs they work 40 hours a week they get their girls to all their sporting events one way or another they are very active helping the girls with their school work they have a great family life yet they both workout at the gym how is that 40 hour work weeks raising 2 young girls those girls playing 2 3 sports at a time and yet they still train 4 5 days a week they still take time to cook and eat home cooked meals they still make time to take care of their bodies and you can see it right here here in holly s transformation holly could easily say she s tired she could easily use the excuse that she don t have time she could easily sit home and relax but she doesn t she gets her ass in the gym and works hard it s all about what you want do you want to reach your goals or do you want to continue making excuses for why you didn t great job holly you re killing it and your transformation is incredible you should be very proud of

a dosa is a cooked flat thin layered rice batter originating from the indian subcontinent made from a fermented batter it is somewhat similar to a crepe in appearance its main ingredients are rice and black gram ground together in a fine smooth batter with a dash of salt dosas are a typical part of the southern indian and sri lankan tamil diets but the dish is now popular all over the indian subcontinent traditionally dosas are served hot along with sambar a stuffing of potatoes and chutney they can be consumed with idli as
